SELECT COUNT(*)
  FROM (
        SELECT DISTINCT "app_table"."id" AS "col1",
               "app_table"."tempo_seconds" AS "col2"
          FROM "app_table"
         INNER JOIN "app_hand"
            ON ("app_table"."id" = "app_hand"."table_id")
         WHERE "app_hand"."id" IN (
                SELECT DISTINCT V0."id"
                  FROM "app_hand" V0
                 WHERE V0."board_id" IN (
                        SELECT U0."id"
                          FROM "app_board" U0
                         WHERE U0."tournament_id" = 1
                       )
               )
       ) subquery

SELECT "app_seat"."id",
       "app_seat"."direction",
       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 8 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'N')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 5 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'W')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 9 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'N')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

       "app_seat"."direction",
       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 4 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'W')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 1 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'E')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

SELECT "app_seat"."id",
       "app_seat"."direction",
       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 6 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'N')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

SELECT "app_seat"."id",
       "app_seat"."direction",
       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 8 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'N')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

Execution time: 0.000703s [Database: default]
SELECT "app_seat"."id",
       "app_seat"."direction",
       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 7 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'N')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

       "app_seat"."player_id",
       "app_seat"."table_id",
       "app_player"."id",
       "app_player"."user_id",
       "app_player"."partner_id",
       "app_player"."currently_seated",
       "auth_user"."id",
       "auth_user"."password",
       "auth_user"."last_login",
       "auth_user"."is_superuser",
       "auth_user"."username",
       "auth_user"."first_name",
       "auth_user"."last_name",
       "auth_user"."email",
       "auth_user"."is_staff",
       "auth_user"."is_active",
       "auth_user"."date_joined"
  FROM "app_seat"
 INNER JOIN "app_player"
    ON ("app_seat"."player_id" = "app_player"."id")
 INNER JOIN "auth_user"
    ON ("app_player"."user_id" = "auth_user"."id")
 WHERE ("app_seat"."table_id" = 6 AND "app_seat"."direction" = 'S')
 ORDER BY (position(DIRECTION in 'NESW')) ASC
 LIMIT 1

SELECT COUNT(*)
  FROM (
        SELECT DISTINCT "app_table"."id" AS "col1",
               "app_table"."tempo_seconds" AS "col2"
          FROM "app_table"
         INNER JOIN "app_hand"
            ON ("app_table"."id" = "app_hand"."table_id")
         WHERE "app_hand"."id" IN (
                SELECT DISTINCT V0."id"
                  FROM "app_hand" V0
                 WHERE V0."board_id" IN (
                        SELECT U0."id"
                          FROM "app_board" U0
                         WHERE U0."tournament_id" = 1
                       )
               )
       ) subquery

               "app_table"."tempo_seconds" AS "col2"

            ON ("app_table"."id" = "app_hand"."table_id")

         INNER JOIN "app_hand"
            ON ("app_table"."id" = "app_hand"."table_id")
         WHERE "app_hand"."id" IN (
                SELECT DISTINCT V0."id"
                  FROM "app_hand" V0
                 WHERE V0."board_id" IN (
                        SELECT U0."id"
                          FROM "app_board" U0
                         WHERE U0."tournament_id" = 2
                       )
               )
       ) subquery
